 3-Step Linear Workflow

================================================================================
                              KEY PATTERNS
================================================================================

Burr ApplicationBuilder:
  app = (
      ApplicationBuilder()
      .with_actions(action1=action1, action2=action2)
      .with_transitions(("action1", "action2"))
      .with_state_persister(persister)
      .with_tracker(tracker)
      .with_identifiers(app_id=uuid, partition_key=uuid)
      .build()
  )

Action Decorator:
  @action(reads=["field1"], writes=["field2"])
  async def my_action(state: State, param: str) -> State:
      value = state["field1"]
      result = await process(value, param)
      return state.update(field2=result)

Async Execution:
  action, result, state = await app.arun(
      halt_after=["action_name"],
      inputs={"param": "value"}
  )
